# Status

Last update: 2026-02-23
- Closed the Apalache formal-model liveness gap in `docs/formal/sumeragi/Sumeragi.tla`: added explicit enable predicates and post-GST scheduler guards so `TimeoutTick` and `ByzantineFault` cannot preempt enabled non-timeout progress actions (`Honest*` and `Rbc*` progress), eliminating the previous post-GST starvation/no-op lasso counterexample.
- Revalidated formal tiers with a local Apalache 0.52.2 binary (`APALACHE_BIN=/tmp/apalache_0_52_2_U1hAQV/apalache/bin/apalache-mc`): `bash scripts/formal/sumeragi_apalache.sh fast` (ok, `NoError`, bounded length 10, `72.367s`) and `bash scripts/formal/sumeragi_apalache.sh deep` (ok, `NoError`, bounded length 10, `34.362s`). Also updated `docs/formal/sumeragi/README.md` to document operational fairness encoding in `Next` because Apalache 0.52.x does not support `WF_` fairness operators inside checked temporal properties.
- Added explicit regression coverage for the fair-scheduler timeout-preemption guard in `crates/iroha_core/src/sumeragi/main_loop/tests/state_machine_fairness_model_tests.rs`: `fair_scheduler_allows_timeout_before_gst_but_blocks_it_after_gst_when_progress_is_enabled` and `fair_scheduler_timeout_step_keeps_honest_progress_debt_when_it_preempts_enabled_event`. - No-roster starvation root-cause hardening landed in Sumeragi recovery (`crates/iroha_core/src/sumeragi/main_loop{.rs,/votes.rs,/commit.rs,/reschedule.rs,/tests.rs}`): added explicit per-(height,view) roster bootstrap state (`RosterReady`/`RosterBootstrapPending`/`RosterBootstrapExhausted`), deterministic pre-fail-closed bootstrap reacquire ordering (highest-QC fetch, parent-gap fetch, anchor range-pull, commit-topology refresh), and a deterministic refresh-then-single-fallback allowance per view before fail-closed escalation. No-roster fallback budgeting is now timeout-aware via `effective_no_roster_fallback_views = clamp(1..cap, ceil(quorum_timeout/propose_timeout))` with cap from config; fail-closed remains safety-first and once-per-view. Updated no-roster fallback call sites in commit/vote/reschedule paths to handle `AllowFallback` vs `BootstrapPending` vs `FailClosed`, added regression coverage for pending-window suppression prevention, and exposed `consensus_no_roster_fallback_total`, `consensus_no_roster_fallback_allowed_total`, and `consensus_no_roster_fail_closed_total` in Torii status JSON (`crates/iroha_torii/src/routing/consensus.rs`). Tuned Izanami fast profile recovery knobs (`crates/izanami/src/chaos.rs`) with explicit deterministic values: `missing_qc_reacquire_window_ms=450`, `no_roster_fallback_views=2`, `no_roster_refresh_retry_per_view=2`. - Offline settlement atomicity hardening (`crates/iroha_core/src/smartcontracts/isi/offline.rs`): fixed `SubmitOfflineToOnlineTransfer` so allowance mutation (`remaining_amount`, commitment, counter state) and transfer-record insertion happen only after `credit_deposit_account` succeeds, preventing failed escrow credit from decrementing offline allowance state. Hardened `credit_deposit_account` with destination-account preflight checks and escrow refund-on-deposit-failure protection, and made post-credit settlement writes infallible (precomputed `receipt_count`, infallible transfer-event emission/record insertion after prevalidation) to avoid partial post-credit rejection paths. Added regressions `submit_transfer_rejects_insufficient_escrow_without_mutating_allowance_or_credit` and `credit_deposit_account_rejects_missing_deposit_without_escrow_debit` to lock in no-debit/no-credit behavior across escrow shortfall and missing-deposit-account failures. - Torii/client queue rejection decoding + NPoS stress test de-flake (`crates/iroha_torii_shared/src/lib.rs`, `crates/iroha_torii/src/lib.rs`, `crates/iroha/src/client.rs`, `integration_tests/tests/sumeragi_npos_performance.rs`): introduced shared Norito queue-rejection payload types (`QueueErrorEnvelope`, `QueueErrorSnapshot`) in `iroha_torii_shared` and switched Torii + client to those shared types so client-side `ResponseReport` can decode `429 PRTRY:QUEUE_FULL` Norito payloads instead of reporting "body isn't a valid utf-8 string". Added client/unit coverage (`with_msg_decodes_shared_queue_error_envelope`) and shared-type roundtrip coverage. Together these tests assert decentralized semantics end-to-end via `/v1/connect/status`: broadcast+P2P rebroadcasts over node-to-node transport, broadcast-without-P2P degrades to local-only with skipped counters (no centralized fallback), unknown strategies remain local-only even with attached P2P, and both `local_only` and `relay_enabled=false` never rebroadcast even when P2P is attached. JS SDK coverage now includes `getConnectStatus preserves relay-disabled effective local-only fields`, while Connect docs now clarify status JSON fields (`p2p_rebroadcasts_total`, `p2p_rebroadcast_skipped_total`) vs telemetry metric names and call out the relay-disabled effective-local-only case in the JS guide. - Iroha Connect hardening (Torii + SDKs): enforced strict contiguous per-direction sequence policy with session termination on violations (`connect_sequence_violation`), enforced role→direction validation at WS ingress (`connect_role_direction_mismatch`), added new Connect status counters, and added relay strategy hardening (`broadcast` vs `local_only`, unknown values forced to `local_only`) so relay behavior stays node-to-node on the Iroha P2P network without introducing centralized relay modes. JS queue journal now drops corrupted entries instead of failing decode paths, and JS connect error mapping now treats `HTTP 408/429` as retryable timeout/transport classes instead of broad auth errors. Python Connect codec loading now fails closed by default when the native extension is unavailable (stub requires explicit `IROHA_PYTHON_CONNECT_CODEC=stub`), and the Python stub codec replaced `pickle` payloads with deterministic JSON+base64url encoding. Swift `ConnectSession` mutable state is synchronized and flow-control consumption now happens only after key presence/decrypt success, with new concurrency and flow-control regression tests. Key changes: (1) reschedule now uses progress stall age, defers near-quorum churn while `rbc_chunk_rx` is active, and only forces reassembly after availability timeout; (2) idle view-change now grants an RBC-progress grace window after timeout when backlog is still converging; (3) missing-block fetch retry windows widen when RBC session progress is observed; (4) block-sync locked-chain conflicts are prefiltered and warning-throttled under a dedicated conflict kind; (5) ahead-of-tip pending blocks defer validation and request missing parents before static validation dispatch. - `iroha_core`/`iroha_config`/`iroha_data_model` production STARK backend (`crates/iroha_core/src/{zk_stark.rs,zk.rs,smartcontracts/isi/world.rs,pipeline/overlay.rs}`, `crates/iroha_config/src/parameters/{defaults.rs,user.rs,actual.rs}`, `crates/iroha_data_model/src/zk.rs`, `crates/iroha_torii/src/{lib.rs,zk_prover.rs}`, `crates/iroha_torii/docs/zk_app_api.md`, `docs/source/zk_app_api.md`, `docs/source/zk/lifecycle.md`): enabled deterministic native STARK/FRI verification for `stark/fri-v1/*` (no trusted setup) and wired it into the shared `verify_backend` dispatch while preserving existing Halo2 behavior. STARK verification is runtime-gated via config (`zk.stark.enabled`, `zk.stark.max_proof_bytes`) and expects proof bytes to be a Norito-encoded `OpenVerifyEnvelope` with `BackendTag::Stark` carrying a `StarkFriOpenProofV1` wrapper: higher-level flows (governance voting + `Executable::IvmProved` admission) validate public inputs, and the inner STARK envelope is bound to `(backend, circuit_id, vk_hash, schema descriptor, public inputs)` via a domain-tag digest to prevent re-wrapping. Voting public-input extraction and shielded tx admission now accept `stark/fri-v1/*` alongside `halo2/ipa` when explicitly configured; Torii `/v1/zk/ivm/derive` accepts STARK VKs compatible with `ivm-execution-v1`. - `iroha_core`/`iroha_data_model` proof-carrying IVM execution verification (`crates/iroha_core/src/pipeline/overlay.rs`, `crates/iroha_core/src/zk.rs`, `crates/iroha_data_model/src/transaction/executable.rs`): `Executable::IvmProved` admission now requires `halo2/ipa:ivm-execution-v1` proofs to bind 16 instance columns covering `(code_hash, overlay_hash, events_commitment, gas_policy_commitment)`. The proved bytecode must have the IVM ZK mode bit set (`mode & ZK != 0`). After backend verification, the node typically recomputes the overlay plus commitments by deterministic VM replay and rejects mismatches. The events/gas commitments are derived from a hashed execution trace (no trace-preimage copying), and `gas_policy_commitment` binds a non-public trace hash so the committed `gas_used` cannot be brute-forced without reproducing the trace (no plaintext gas usage is exposed). `ivm-execution-v1` uses a canonical public-input schema descriptor/hash for VK binding (instead of value-dependent schema hashing), while proof instances are validated directly from proof bytes. The legacy `halo2/ipa:ivm-overlay-bind-v1` binding-only stand-in circuit remains explicitly rejected. Replay can be skipped via `pipeline.ivm_proved.skip_replay = true` when a full-semantics proof circuit is accepted.
- `iroha_torii` IVM prove API (`crates/iroha_torii/src/lib.rs`, `crates/iroha_core/src/zk.rs`, `crates/iroha/src/client.rs`, `crates/iroha_cli/src/zk.rs`, `crates/iroha_torii/docs/zk_app_api.md`, `docs/source/zk_app_api.md`, `crates/iroha_config/src/parameters/{defaults.rs,user.rs,actual.rs}`): `POST /v1/zk/ivm/derive` executes IVM bytecode (requires `mode & ZK != 0`) and returns a derived `IvmProved` payload (overlay + commitments only, no plaintext `gas_used`). `POST/GET/DELETE /v1/zk/ivm/prove...` generates a **real** `halo2/ipa` `ivm-execution-v1` proof attachment (no fixture proofs) by loading proving key bytes from `torii.zk_prover_keys_dir/<backend>__<name>.pk` and binding commitments without exposing plaintext `gas_used`. The endpoint can also load verifying key bytes from `torii.zk_prover_keys_dir/<backend>__<name>.vk` when the registry entry omits inline VK bytes. Prove job processing is bounded by `torii.zk_ivm_prove_max_inflight` + `torii.zk_ivm_prove_max_queue` (saturated requests get `429` + `Retry-After`), and job retention is configurable via `torii.zk_ivm_prove_job_ttl_secs` + `torii.zk_ivm_prove_job_max_entries` (TTL eviction cancels pending/running jobs best-effort to free permits). Job status values are `pending|running|done|error`; `DELETE` triggers best-effort cancellation (queued jobs release capacity immediately; in-flight proving is not preemptible). Telemetry exports `torii_zk_ivm_prove_inflight` and `torii_zk_ivm_prove_queued` gauges. Added `iroha_core::zk::derive_halo2_ipa_ivm_execution_proving_key_bytes` plus CLI helpers (`iroha app zk ivm derive`, `iroha app zk ivm ...`, `iroha app zk ivm derive-pk`) and `iroha::client::Client` JSON wrappers for these endpoints. Validation: `cargo fmt --all` (ok), `cargo test -p iroha_torii zk_ivm_prove_ -- --nocapture` (ok), `cargo test -p iroha_cli -- --nocapture` (ok), `cargo test -p iroha zk_ivm_prove_ -- --nocapture` (ok), `cargo test -p iroha_config -- --nocapture` (ok).
- `iroha_test_network` async binary resolution + startup-diagnostics test hardening (`crates/iroha_test_network/src/lib.rs`): added `Program::resolve_async()` (wraps the existing resolver in `tokio::task::spawn_blocking`) and switched network startup paths to use it so nested `cargo build` and filesystem probing cannot block Tokio runtime threads (which can starve timers and appear as “hung” tests). Added 20-minute `tokio::time::timeout` guards around `Program::Irohad.resolve_async()` in `tests::can_start_networks` and `tests::starts_single_peer_with_minimal_genesis_fallback`, and guarded the `startup_diagnostics_*` unit tests with `skip_network_tests(...)` (they still allocate ports). Also serialized the env-override resolver test under `PROGRAM_BIN_ENV_GUARD` and added `tests::program_resolve_async_honors_env_override`. - `iroha_core` runtime-upgrade admission hash check (`crates/iroha_core/src/tx.rs`): during IVM transaction admission, if a runtime-upgrade record is `ActivatedAt(h)` for the program's ABI version, require the program's computed `abi_hash` to match the active manifest (reject mismatches with `IvmAdmissionError::ManifestAbiHashMismatch`). This fixes `runtime_upgrade_admission::active_manifest_hash_mismatch_rejects_contracts` accepting tampered manifests. - IVM/DefaultHost numeric syscalls: fixed Norito format drift in `crates/ivm/src/host.rs` by decoding numeric pointers via `norito::decode_from_bytes::<Numeric>` and encoding all numeric syscall outputs with `norito::to_bytes` (instead of raw `Numeric::decode`/`Numeric::encode`). This restores parity with `CoreHost`/`WsvHost` and brings `numeric_syscalls` expectations (`AssertionFailed` vs decode failures, numeric payload decodeability) back in line. Validation: `cargo test -p ivm --test numeric_syscalls -- --nocapture` (ok; 12 passed), `cargo fmt --all` (ok; stable rustfmt emitted existing nightly-option warnings).
- IVM runtime host wrapper: fixed `set_host()` regression where `runtime::SyscallDispatcher` dropped `access_logging_supported()` and caused declared-access transactions to fail before execution. Added forwarding for `access_logging_supported()` in both `SyscallDispatcher<H>` and `SharedHost` (`crates/ivm/src/runtime.rs`), restoring access-log-aware block execution in sequential and shared-host paths. Validation: `cargo test -p ivm --test parallel block_succeeds_with_logged_state_writes_committed -- --nocapture` (ok), `cargo test -p ivm --test parallel -- --nocapture` (ok; 20 passed), `cargo fmt --all` (ok; stable rustfmt emitted existing nightly-option warnings).
- IVM/DefaultHost numeric syscalls (follow-up): re-applied Norito parity in `crates/ivm/src/host.rs` after regression where numeric payloads were encoded/decoded with raw `Numeric::encode`/`Numeric::decode` again. `decode_numeric` now uses `norito::decode_from_bytes::<Numeric>`, and all numeric syscall outputs use `norito::to_bytes`, restoring expected assertion semantics and decodable `NoritoBytes` payloads in `numeric_syscalls`. Validation: `cargo test -p ivm --test numeric_syscalls -- --nocapture` (ok; 12 passed), `cargo fmt --all` (ok; stable rustfmt emitted existing nightly-option warnings).
- IVM pointer TLV tests: updated stale pointer-ABI fixture literals in `crates/ivm/tests/pointer_tlv.rs` to current parser expectations (`AccountId` in multihash form and `NftId` in `name$domain` form) so payload normalization in `crates/ivm/tests/common.rs` no longer panics before TLV validation checks run.
